Intelligence\nexport type AudioState = 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'SPEAKING' | 'PAUSED';\nexport type VoiceMode = 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text';\n\nconst WORD_TO_DIGIT: Record<string, string> = {\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\s+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    } else if (/^\\d$/.test(word)) {\n      digits += word;\n    }\n  }\n  return digits || text.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n};\n\nexport const formatPhone = (digits: string): string => {\n  const d = digits.slice(0, 10);\n  if (d.length <= 3) return d;\n  if (d.length <= 6) return `${d.slice(0, 3)}-${d.slice(3)}`;\n  return `${d.slice(0, 3)}-${d.slice(3, 6)}-${d.slice(6)}`;\n};\n\ninterface BrainState {\n  audioState: AudioState;\n  mode: VoiceMode;\n  transcript: string;\n  context: string;\n  error: string | null;\n}\n\nclass VoiceBrainClass {\n  private static instance: VoiceBrainClass;\n  private recognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\n  private synth: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\n  \n  private state: BrainState = {\n    audioState: 'IDLE',\n    mode: 'interactive',\n    transcript: '',\n    context: '',\n    error: null\n  };\n  \n  private listeners = new private initialized = false;\n\n  static getInstance(): VoiceBrainClass {\n    if (!VoiceBrainClass.instance) {\n      VoiceBrainClass.instance = new VoiceBrainClass();\n    }\n    return VoiceBrainClass.instance;\n  }\n\n  init(): boolean {\n    if (this.initialized) return true;\n    \n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.' });\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\n    this.recognition = new SR();\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\n\n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Listening...');\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'LISTENING', error: null });\n    };\n\n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\n      \n      if (result.isFinal && text) {\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text });\n        this.processText(text.toLowerCase());\n      }\n    };\n\n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\n        this.updateState({ error: 'Microphone blocked. Allow in browser settings.', audioState: 'IDLE' });\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\n      }\n    };\n\n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else if (this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\n        this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n      }\n    };\n\n    this.initialized = true;\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Initialized');\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  private updateState(partial: Partial<BrainState>): void {\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\n  }\n\n  private processText(text: string): void {\n    // Pause commands\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text === 'stop' || text === 'pause') {\n      this.pause();\n      this.speak(\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume to continue.\");\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Resume\n    if (text === 'resume' || text === 'continue') {\n      this.resume();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Extract digits\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\n    if (digits) {\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\n    }\n\n    // Send to command handlers\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\n  }\n\n  getState(): BrainState {\n    return { ...this.state };\n  }\n\n  subscribe(listener: (state: BrainState) => void): () => void {\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\n    listener(this.state);\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\n  }\n\n  onDigits(handler: (digits: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n\n  onCommand(handler: (cmd: string) => void): () => void {\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n\n  setContext(context: string): void {\n    this.updateState({ context });\n  }\n\n  setMode(mode: VoiceMode): void {\n    this.updateState({ mode });\n  }\n\n  start(): void {\n    if (!this.init()) return;\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') return;\n    \n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n    }\n  }\n\n  stop(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n    }\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n  }\n\n  pause(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n    }\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'PAUSED' });\n  }\n\n  resume(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n    }\n    this.speak(\"I'm listening.\");\n  }\n\n  speak(text: string, onDone?: () => void): void {\n    if (!text || this.state.mode === 'text') {\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!this.init() || !this.synth) {\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Stop listening while speaking (Audio Mutex)\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\n    }\n\n    this.synth.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'SPEAKING' });\n\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1;\n    utterance.pitch = 1;\n    utterance.volume = 1;\n\n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US'));\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n\n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n\n    utterance.onerror = () => {\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n      onDone?.();\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n\n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\n  }\n}\n\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrainClass.getInstance();\nexport default voiceBrain;\nENDFILE\n\necho \"  \u2705 VoiceBrain.ts\"\n\n# --- AgenticBar.tsx ---\ncat > \"$W/src/agentic/AgenticBar.tsx\" << 'ENDFILE'\n// 'five': '5',\\n  'six': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const word of words) {\\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) {\\n      digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\\n    } else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(word)) {\\n      digits += word;\\n    }\\n  }\\n  return digits || text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n};\\n\\nexport const formatPhone = (digits: string): string => {\\n  const d = digits.slice(0, 10);\\n  if (d.length <= 3) return d;\\n  if (d.length <= 6) return `${d.slice(0, 3)}-${d.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${d.slice(0, 3)}-${d.slice(3, 6)}-${d.slice(6)}`;\\n};\\n\\ninterface BrainState {\\n  audioState: AudioState;\\n  mode: VoiceMode;\\n  transcript: string;\\n  context: string;\\n  error: string | null;\\n}\\n\\nclass VoiceBrainClass {\\n  private static instance: VoiceBrainClass;\\n  private Allow in browser settings.', audioState: 'IDLE' });\\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\\n            try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n          }\\n        }, 100);\\n      } else if (this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    this.initialized = true;\\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Initialized');\\n    return true;\\n  }\\n\\n  private updateState(partial: Partial<BrainState>): void {\\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\\n  }\\n\\n  private processText(text: string): void {\\n    // Pause commands\\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text === 'stop' || text === 'pause') {\\n      this.pause();\\n      this.speak(\\\"I'm here when you need me. this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\\n  }\\n\\n  getState(): BrainState {\\n    return { ...this.state };\\n  }\\n\\n  subscribe(listener: (state: BrainState) => void): () => void {\\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\\n    listener(this.state);\\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\\n  }\\n\\n  onDigits(handler: (digits: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n\\n  onCommand(handler: (cmd: string) => void): () => void {\\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\\n this.updateState({ mode });\\n  }\\n\\n  start(): void {\\n    if (!this.init()) return;\\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') return;\\n    \\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n    }\\n  }\\n\\n  stop(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\\n  }\\n\\n  pause(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'PAUSED' });\\n  }\\n\\n  resume(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n    }\\n    this.speak(\\\"I'm listening.\\\");\\n  }\\n\\n  speak(text: string, onDone?: () => void): void {\\n    if (!text || this.state.mode === 'text') {\\n      onDone?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (!this.init() || !this.synth) {\\n      onDone?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n\\n    // Stop listening while speaking (Audio Mutex)\\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\n    }\\n\\n    this.synth.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'SPEAKING' });\\n\\n    const utterance = new this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    setTimeout(() => this.synth?.speak(utterance), 50);\\n  }\\n}\\n\\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrainClass.getInstance();\\nexport default Welcome aboard.', () => onVerified());\\n    } else {\\n      setError('Invalid code. Demo code is 123456');\\n      speak('Invalid code. For demo, say one two three four five six.');\\n    }\\n  }, [onVerified]);\\n\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    setOtp(prev => {\\n      const filled = prev.filter(d => d).length;\\n      const next = [...prev];\\n      let idx = filled;\\n\\n      for (const d of digits) {\\n        if (idx < 6) {\\n          next[idx] = d;\\n          idx++;\\n        }\\n      }\\n\\n      if (next.filter(d => d).length === 6) {\\n        setTimeout(() => verifyCode(next.join('')), 300);\\n      }\\n\\n      return next;\\n    });\\n  }, [verifyCode]);\\n\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset')) {\\n      setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\\n      setError('');\\n      speak('Cleared. Enter the code again.');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const u1 = onDigits(handleDigits);\\n    const u2 = onCommand(handleCommand);\\n    return () => { u1(); u2(); };\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\\n\\n  const handleInput = (index: number, value: string) => {\\n    if (!/^\\\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\\n    const next = [...otp];\\n    next[index] = value.slice(-1);\\n    setOtp(next);\\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\\n    if (next.every(d => d)) verifyCode(next.join(''));\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udd10</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n        Verification Code\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Code sent to {phone}\\n      </p>\\n\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\\n          <input\\n            key={idx}\\n            ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el}\\n            type=\\\"text\\\"\\n            inputMode=\\\"numeric\\\"\\n            maxLength={1}\\n            value={digit}\\n            onChange={e => handleInput(idx, e.target.value)}\\n            style={{\\n              width: '55px',\\n              height: '68px',\\n              fontSize: '2em',\\n              textAlign: 'center',\\n              borderRadius: '12px',\\n              border: `3px solid ${digit ?  \\n    this.synth.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ state: 'SPEAKING' });\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = useCallback } from 'react';\\nimport { voiceService, extractDigits, formatPhone } from '../services/voiceService';\\n\\nexport { extractDigits, formatPhone };\\n\\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n}\\n\\nexport function useVoice(options: UseVoiceOptions = {}) {\\n  const { onDigits, onCommand, voiceService.init();\\n    return voiceService.subscribe(setState);\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  // Register digit handler\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (onDigits) {\\n      return }\\n  }, [onCommand]);\\n  \\n  // Auto-start listening\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      voiceService.startListening();\\n    }\\n  }, [autoStart]);\\n  \\n  return {\\n    isListening: state.state === 'LISTENING',\\n    isSpeaking: state.state === 'SPEAKING',\\n    isPaused: state.state === 'PAUSED',\\n    transcript: state.transcript,\\n    interimTranscript: state.interimTranscript,\\n    error: state.error,\\n    start: useCallback(() => voiceService.startListening(), []),\\n    stop: useCallback(() => voiceService.stopListening(), []),\\n    speak: Uses unified AgenticBar\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\\nimport { useVoice, extractDigits, formatPhone } from '../../../hooks/useVoice';\\nimport AgenticBar from '../../AgenticBar';\\nimport { voiceService } from '../../../services/voiceService';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  value: string;\\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\\n  onNext: () => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ value, onChange, onNext }) => {\\n  const [digits, setDigits] = useState(value.replace(/\\\\D/g, ''));\\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\\n  const voice = useVoice({ autoStart: false });\\n  \\n  // Handle digits from voice\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((newDigits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorPhone] Digits:', newDigits);\\n    setDigits(prev => {\\n      const updated = (prev + newDigits).slice(0, 10);\\n      onChange(updated);\\n      \\n      if (updated.length === 10) {\\n        voiceService.speak(`Got it! ${formatPhone(updated)}. Say yes to confirm, or clear to reset.`);\\n      } else if (newDigits) {\\n        voiceService.speak(`${10 - updated.length} more.`);\\n      }\\n      return updated;\\n    });\\n  }, [onChange]);\\n  \\n  // Handle commands\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorPhone] Command:', cmd);\\n    \\n    if ((cmd.includes('yes') || cmd.includes('confirm') || cmd.includes('send') || cmd.includes('correct')) && digits.length >= 10) {\\n      voiceService.speak('Sending verification code.', () => onNext());\\n    }\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset') || cmd.includes('start over')) {\\n      setDigits('');\\n      onChange('');\\n      voiceService.speak('Cleared. Say your number again.');\\n    }\\n  }, [digits, onChange, onNext]);\\n  \\n  // Register handlers\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const unsubDigits = voiceService.onDigits(handleDigits);\\n    const unsubCommand = voiceService.onCommand(handleCommand);\\n    return () => { unsubDigits(); unsubCommand(); };\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\\n  \\n  // Welcome + auto-start\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current) {\\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\\n      voiceService.init();\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voiceService.speak('Welcome to VistaView! Say your phone number. Like seven zero three.', () => {\\n          voiceService.startListening();\\n        });\\n      }, 500);\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  // Sync with prop\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const cleaned = value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (cleaned !== digits) setDigits(cleaned);\\n  }, [value]);\\n  \\n  const canSubmit = digits.length >= 10;\\n  \\n  return (\\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\\ud83d\\udcf1</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\\n        Enter Your Phone Number\\n      </h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Say digits like \\\"seven zero three\\\" or type below\\n      </p>\\n      \\n      {/* Phone Input */}\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '1.5em' }}>+1</span>\\n        <input\\n          type=\\\"tel\\\"\\n          value={formatPhone(digits)}\\n          onChange={e => {\\n            const clean = e.target.value.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n            setDigits(clean);\\n            onChange(clean);\\n          }}\\n          placeholder=\\\"000-000-0000\\\"\\n          style={{\\n            fontSize: '2em', padding: '18px 28px', borderRadius: '14px',\\n            border: `3px solid ${canSubmit ? '#4CAF50' : 'rgba(184,134,11,0.4)'}`,\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', color: '#fff', textAlign: 'center',\\n            width: '300px', fontFamily: 'monospace', letterSpacing: '3px'\\n          }}\\n        />\\n        {digits && (\\n          <button onClick={() => { setDigits(''); onChange(''); voiceService.speak('Cleared.'); }}\\n            style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', border: 'none', color: '#888',\\n              width: '40px', height: '40px', borderRadius: '50%', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '1.2em' }}>\\n            \\u2715\\n          </button>\\n        )}\\n      </div>\\n      \\n      {canSubmit && (\\n        <p style={{ color: '#4CAF50', marginBottom: '16px', fontWeight: 500 }}>\\n          \\u2713 Phone complete! Say \\\"yes\\\" to confirm\\n        </p>\\n      )}\\n      \\n      {/* Submit Button */}\\n      <button\\n        onClick={() => canSubmit && voiceService.speak('Sending code.', () => onNext())}\\n        disabled={!canSubmit}\\n        style={{\\n          padding: '16px 52px',\\n          background: canSubmit ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed', fontSize: '1.1em', fontWeight: 700,\\n          boxShadow: canSubmit ? Uses unified AgenticBar\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';\\nimport AgenticBar from '../../AgenticBar';\\nimport { voiceService } from '../../../services/voiceService';\\n\\ninterface Props {\\n  phone: string;\\n  onVerified: () => void;\\n}\\n\\nconst VendorOTP: React.FC<Props> = ({ phone, onVerified }) => {\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState<string[]>(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\\n  const [error, setError] = useState('');\\n  const inputRefs = useRef<(HTMLInputElement | null)[]>([]);\\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\\n  \\n  const verifyCode = useCallback((code: string) => {\\n    if (code === '123456') {\\n      voiceService.speak('Verified! Welcome aboard.', () => onVerified());\\n    } else {\\n      setError('Invalid code. Demo: 123456');\\n      voiceService.speak('Invalid code. The demo code is one two three four five six.');\\n    }\\n  }, [onVerified]);\\n  \\n  // Handle digits\\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\\n    console.log('[VendorOTP] Digits:', digits);\\n    setOtp(prev => {\\n      const filled = prev.filter(d => d).length;\\n      const next = [...prev];\\n      let idx = filled;\\n      for (const d of digits) {\\n        if (idx < 6) { next[idx] = d; idx++; }\\n      }\\n      if (next.filter(d => d).length === 6) {\\n        setTimeout(() => verifyCode(next.join('')), 300);\\n      }\\n      return next;\\n    });\\n  }, [verifyCode]);\\n  \\n  // Handle commands\\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset')) {\\n      setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\\n      setError('');\\n      voiceService.speak('Cleared.');\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n  \\n  // Register handlers\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const unsubDigits = voiceService.onDigits(handleDigits);\\n    const unsubCommand = voiceService.onCommand(handleCommand);\\n    return () => { unsubDigits(); unsubCommand(); };\\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\\n  \\n  // Welcome\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current) {\\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\\n      setTimeout(() => {\\n        voiceService.speak('Enter the 6 digit code. Created ${result.stats?.totalProducts || 0} products from your catalog.   <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\\n        Upload a PDF catalog to create your product listings\\n      </p>\\n\\n      {state.status === 'idle' && (\\n        <>\\n \\ud83d\\udcc1 Choose PDF File\\n          </button>\\n          <p style={{ color: '#666', marginTop: '16px', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\n            or drag and drop your PDF here\\n          </p>\\n any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (!SR) {\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Click \ud83d\udd12 in address bar \u2192 Allow' \n        });\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\n      } else if (event.error !== 'no-speech' && event.error !== 'aborted') {\n        this.updateState({ error: `Error: ${event.error}` });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Ended, shouldRestart:', this.shouldRestart, 'state:', this.state.audioState);\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\n            try { \n              this.recognition.start(); \n            } catch (e) { \n              console.log('[VoiceBrain] Restart failed:', e);\n            }\n          }\n        }, 100);\n      } else if (this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\n        this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n      }\n    };\n    \n    this.initialized = true;\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] \u2705 Initialized');\n    return true;\n  }\n  \n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  // STATE MANAGEMENT\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  private updateState(partial: Partial<BrainState>): void {\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\n  }\n  \n  getState(): BrainState {\n    return { ...this.state };\n  }\n  \n  subscribe(listener: StateListener): () => void {\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\n    listener(this.state);\n    return () => this.listeners.delete(listener);\n  }\n  \n  onDigits(handler: DigitHandler): () => void {\n    this.digitHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.digitHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  onCommand(handler: CommandHandler): () => void {\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\n  }\n  \n  setContext(context: string): void {\n    this.updateState({ context });\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Context:', context);\n  }\n  \n  setMode(mode: VoiceMode): void {\n    this.updateState({ mode });\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Mode:', mode);\n  }\n  \n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  // TEXT PROCESSING\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  private processText(text: string): void {\n    // Pause commands\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text === 'stop' || text === 'pause' || text.includes('wait')) {\n      this.pause();\n      this.speak(\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume to continue.\");\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Resume commands\n    if (text === 'resume' || text === 'continue' || text === 'go ahead') {\n      this.resume();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Mode switching\n    if (text.includes('talkative mode')) {\n      this.setMode('talkative');\n      this.speak('Talkative mode. I will give more details.');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (text.includes('text mode') || text.includes('silent')) {\n      this.setMode('text');\n      this.speak('Text mode. I will stay quiet.');\n      return;\n    }\n    if (text.includes('interactive mode')) {\n      this.setMode('interactive');\n      this.speak('Interactive mode.');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Extract digits\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\n    if (digits) {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Digits:', digits);\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\n    }\n    \n    // Dispatch to command handlers\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\n  }\n  \n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  // AUDIO CONTROL (with Mutex)\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  start(): void {\n    if (!this.init()) return;\n    \n    // Audio Mutex: Don't start listening if speaking\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Cannot start while speaking');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { \n        this.recognition.start(); \n      } catch (e) { \n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Start error (may already be running):', e);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  stop(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n  }\n  \n  pause(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'PAUSED' });\n  }\n  \n  resume(): void {\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'LISTENING' });\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n    this.speak(\"I'm listening.\");\n  }\n  \n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  // TEXT-TO-SPEECH (with Mutex)\n  // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  speak(text: string, onDone?: () => void): void {\n    if (!text) {\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Text mode = silent\n    if (this.state.mode === 'text') {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Text mode, skipping TTS:', text);\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    if (!this.init() || !this.synth) {\n      onDone?.();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speaking:', text);\n    \n    // AUDIO MUTEX: Stop listening while speaking\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\n    if (this.recognition) {\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n    \n    // Cancel any ongoing speech\n    this.synth.cancel();\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'SPEAKING' });\n    \n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\n    \n    // Get best voice\n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US') && !v.name.includes('Compact'));\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\n    \n    utterance.onend = () => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speech ended');\n      this.updateState({ audioState: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE' });\n      onDone?.();\n      \n      // Resume listening if was listening before\n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    utterance.onerror = (e) => {\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speech error:', e);\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n      onDone?.();\n      \n      if (wasListening) {\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\n      }\n    };\n    \n    // Small delay then speak\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      if (this.synth) {\n        this.synth.speak(utterance);\n      }\n    }, 50);\n  }\n  \n  stopSpeaking(): void {\n    if (this.synth) {\n      this.synth.cancel();\n    }\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') {\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Export singleton\nexport const voiceBrain = VoiceBrainClass.getInstance();\nexport default voiceBrain;\nVBEOF\n\necho \"  \u2705 VoiceBrain.ts\"\n\n# function useVoice() {\n  const [, forceUpdate] = useState(0);\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    voiceBrain.init();\n    return voiceBrain.subscribe(() => forceUpdate(x => x + 1));\n  }, []);\n\n  const state = voiceBrain.getState();\n  return {\n    ...state,\n    isListening: state.audioState === 'LISTENING',\n    isSpeaking: state.audioState === 'SPEAKING',\n    isPaused: state.audioState === 'PAUSED',\n    isIdle: state.audioState === 'IDLE',\n    start: () => voiceBrain.start(),\n    stop: () => voiceBrain.stop(),\n    pause: () => voiceBrain.pause(),\n    resume: () => voiceBrain.resume(),\n    speak: (text: string, onDone?: () => void) => voiceBrain.speak(text, onDone),\n    stopSpeaking: () => voiceBrain.stopSpeaking(),\n    setMode: (mode: VoiceMode) => voiceBrain.setMode(mode),\n    setContext: (ctx: string) => voiceBrain.setContext(ctx)\n  };\n}\n\n// AgenticBar: React.FC<AgenticBarProps> = ({\n  context,\n  hints,\n  welcomeMessage,\n  autoStart = true,\n  showTypeInput = true,\n  onDigits: onDigitsProp,\n  onCommand: onCommandProp\n}) => {\n  const voice = useVoice();\n  const welcomeSpoken = useRef(false);\n  const [textInput, setTextInput] = useState('');\n  const [showModes, setShowModes] = useState(false);\n\n  // Register digit handler\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (onDigitsProp) {\n      return voiceBrain.onDigits(onDigitsProp);\n    }\n  }, [onDigitsProp]);\n\n  // Register command handler\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (onCommandProp) {\n      return voiceBrain.onCommand(onCommandProp);\n    }\n  }, [onCommandProp]);\n\n  // Set context\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (context) {\n      voiceBrain.setContext(context);\n    }\n  }, [context]);\n\n  // Welcome message + auto-start\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!welcomeSpoken.current) {\n      welcomeSpoken.current = true;\n      if (welcomeMessage) {\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          voiceBrain.speak(welcomeMessage, () => {\n            if (autoStart) {\n              voiceBrain.start();\n            }\n          });\n        }, 600);\n      } else if (autoStart) {\n        setTimeout(() => voiceBrain.start(), 500);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [welcomeMessage, autoStart]);\n\n  // Handle text input submit\n  const handleTextSubmit = useCallback(() => {\n    if (textInput.trim()) {\n      const digits = extractDigits(textInput);\n      if (digits && onDigitsProp) {\n        onDigitsProp(digits);\n      }\n      if (onCommandProp) {\n        onCommandProp(textInput.toLowerCase());\n      }\n      setTextInput('');\n    }\n  }, [textInput, onDigitsProp, onCommandProp]);\n\n  // Colors based on state\n  const stateColors: Record<AudioState, string> = {\n    'IDLE': '#666',\n    'LISTENING': '#4CAF50',\n    'SPEAKING': '#FFD700',\n    'PAUSED': '#FF9800'\n  };\n\n  const stateIcons: Record<AudioState, string> = {\n    'IDLE': '\u25a0',\n    'LISTENING': '\ud83c\udfa4',\n    'SPEAKING': '\ud83d\udd0a',\n    'PAUSED': '\u23f8\ufe0f'\n  };\n\n  const statusColor = stateColors[voice.audioState];\n  const statusIcon = stateIcons[voice.audioState];\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{\n      margin: '16px 0 0',\n      padding: '16px',\n      background: `linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(${voice.isListening ? '76,175,80' : voice.isSpeaking ? '255,215,0' : '40,40,40'}, 0.15), rgba(0,0,0,0.3))`,\n      border: `2px solid ${statusColor}`,\n      borderRadius: '16px'\n    }}>\n      {/* Status Row */}\n      <div style={{ \n        display: 'flex', \n        alignItems: 'center', \n        justifyContent: 'space-between', \n        marginBottom: '12px' \n      }}>\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px' }}>\n          <span style={{\n            width: '16px',\n            height: '16px',\n            borderRadius: '50%',\n            background: statusColor,\n            boxShadow: (voice.isListening || voice.isSpeaking) ? `0 0 12px ${statusColor}` : 'none',\n            animation: voice.isListening ? 'agenticPulse 1.5s infinite' : 'none'\n          }} />\n          <span style={{ color: statusColor, fontWeight: 700 }}>\n            {statusIcon} {voice.audioState}\n          </span>\n          {context && (\n            <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>\u2022 {context}</span>\n          )}\n          <span style={{\n            padding: '2px 8px',\n            background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            borderRadius: '10px',\n            fontSize: '0.7em',\n            color: '#aaa',\n            textTransform: 'uppercase'\n          }}>\n            {voice.mode}\n          </span>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Buttons */}\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px', marginBottom: '12px', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>\n        {/* Listen/Stop */}\n        <button\n          onClick={() => voice.isListening ? voice.stop() : voice.start()}\n          style={{\n            padding: '10px 16px',\n            background: voice.isListening ? '#4CAF50' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            color: voice.isListening ? '#fff' : '#aaa',\n            border: voice.isListening ? 'none' : '1px solid #555',\n            borderRadius: '12px',\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            fontWeight: 600\n          }}\n        >\n          \ud83c\udfa4 {voice.isListening ? 'Stop' : 'Listen'}\n        </button>\n\n        {/* Speak Test */}\n        <button\n          onClick={() => voice.speak('Hello! I am Mr. V, your VistaView assistant.')}\n          style={{\n            padding: '10px 16px',\n            background: voice.isSpeaking ? '#FFD700' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',\n            color: voice.isSpeaking ? '#000' : '#aaa',\n            border: voice.isSpeaking ? 'none' : '1px solid #555',\n            borderRadius: '12px',\n            cursor: 'pointer',\n            fontWeight: 600\n          }}\n        >\n          \ud83d\udd0a Speak\n        </button>\n\n        {/* Pause/Resume */}\n        <button\n          onClick={() => voice.isPaused ? voice.resume() : voice.pause()}\n          style={{\n            padding: '10px 16px',\n            background: voice.isPaused ? \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n\\nexport type AudioState = 'IDLE' | 'LISTENING' | 'SPEAKING' | 'PAUSED';\\nexport type VoiceMode = 'interactive' | 'talkative' | 'text';\\n\\n// Word to digit mapping - PROVEN WORKING\\nconst W2D: Record<string, string> = {\\n  'zero': '0', 'oh': '0', 'o': '0',\\n  'one': '1', 'won': '1',\\n  'two': '2', 'to': '2', 'too': '2',\\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4',\\n  'five': '5',\\n  'six': '6',\\n  'seven': '7',\\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\\n  'nine': '9', 'nein': '9'\\n};\\n\\nexport function extractDigits(text: string): string {\\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/\\\\s+/);\\n  let digits = '';\\n  for (const w of words) {\\n    if (W2D[w]) digits += W2D[w];\\n    else if (/^\\\\d$/.test(w)) digits += w;\\n  }\\n  const raw = text.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n  return digits.length >= raw.length ? digits : raw;\\n}\\n\\nexport function formatPhone(d: string): string {\\n  const c = d.replace(/\\\\D/g, '').slice(0, 10);\\n  if (c.length <= 3) return c;\\n  if (c.length <= 6) return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3)}`;\\n  return `${c.slice(0, 3)}-${c.slice(3, 6)}-${c.slice(6)}`;\\n}\\n\\ninterface BrainState {\\n  audioState:  init(): boolean {\\n    if (this.initialized) return true;\\n    \\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Initializing...');\\n    \\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (!SR) {\\n      this.updateState({ error: 'Speech not supported. Use Chrome.' });\\n      console.error('[VoiceBrain] Speech Recognition not supported');\\n      return false;\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.synth = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    this.recognition = new SR();\\n    this.recognition.continuous = true;\\n    this.recognition.interimResults = true;\\n    this.recognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n    this.recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onstart = () => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] \\u2705 LISTENING');\\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'LISTENING', error: null });\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onresult = (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      const result = event.results[event.results.length - 1];\\n      const text = result[0]?.transcript?.trim() || '';\\n      const isFinal = result.isFinal;\\n      \\n      if (isFinal && text) {\\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Heard:', text);\\n        this.updateState({ transcript: text, interim: '' });\\n        this.processText(text.toLowerCase());\\n      } else {\\n        this.updateState({ interim: text });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onerror = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Error:', event.error);\\n      if (event.error === 'not-allowed') {\\n        this.updateState({ \\n          audioState: 'IDLE', \\n          error: 'Microphone blocked. Click \\ud83d\\udd12 in address bar \\u2192 Allow' \\n        });\\n        this.shouldRestart = false;\\n      } else if (event.error !== 'no-speech' && event.error !== 'aborted') {\\n        this.updateState({ error: `Error: ${event.error}` });\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    this.recognition.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Ended, shouldRestart:', this.shouldRestart, 'state:', this.state.audioState);\\n      if (this.shouldRestart && this.state.audioState !== 'SPEAKING' && this.state.audioState !== 'PAUSED') {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (this.shouldRestart && this.recognition) {\\n            try { \\n              this.recognition.start(); \\n            } catch (e) { \\n              console.log('[VoiceBrain] Restart failed:',  private updateState(partial: Partial<BrainState>): void {\\n    this.state = { ...this.state, ...partial };\\n    this.listeners.forEach(l => l(this.state));\\n  }\\n  \\n  getState(): BrainState {\\n    return { ...this.state };\\n  }\\n  \\n  subscribe(listener: StateListener): () => void {\\n    this.listeners.add(listener);\\n    listener(this.state);\\n    return () => \\n  onCommand(handler: CommandHandler): () => void {\\n    this.commandHandlers.add(handler);\\n    return () => this.commandHandlers.delete(handler);\\n  }\\n  \\n  setContext(context: string): void {\\n    this.updateState({ context });\\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Context:', context);\\n  }\\n  \\n  setMode(mode: VoiceMode): void {\\n    this.updateState({ mode });\\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Mode:', mode);\\n  }\\n  \\n  // \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n  private processText(text: string): void {\\n    // Pause commands\\n    if (text.includes('hey') || text === 'stop' || text === 'pause' || text.includes('wait')) {\\n      this.pause();\\n      this.speak(\\\"I'm here when you need me. Say resume to continue.\\\");\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Resume commands\\n    if (text === 'resume' || text === 'continue' || text === 'go ahead') {\\n      this.resume();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Mode switching\\n    if (text.includes('talkative mode')) {\\n      this.setMode('talkative');\\n      this.speak('Talkative mode. I will give more details.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (text.includes('text mode') || text.includes('silent')) {\\n      this.setMode('text');\\n      this.speak('Text mode. I will stay quiet.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    if (text.includes('interactive mode')) {\\n      this.setMode('interactive');\\n      this.speak('Interactive mode.');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Extract digits\\n    const digits = extractDigits(text);\\n    if (digits) {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Digits:', digits);\\n      this.digitHandlers.forEach(h => h(digits));\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Dispatch to command handlers\\n    this.commandHandlers.forEach(h => h(text));\\n  }\\n  \\n  // \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n  // AUDIO CONTROL (with Mutex)\\n  // \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n  start(): void {\\n    if (!this.init()) return;\\n    \\n    // Audio Mutex: Don't start listening if speaking\\n    if (this.state.audioState === 'SPEAKING') {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Cannot start while speaking');\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { \\n        this.recognition.start(); \\n      } catch (e) { \\n        console.log('[VoiceBrain] Start error (may already be running):', e);\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }\\n  \\n  stop(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  pause(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'PAUSED' });\\n  }\\n  \\n  resume(): void {\\n    this.shouldRestart = true;\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'LISTENING' });\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.start(); } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n    this.speak(\\\"I'm listening.\\\");\\n  }\\n  \\n  // \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n  // TEXT-TO-SPEECH (with Mutex)\\n  // \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\n  speak(text: string, onDone?: () => void): void {\\n    if (!text) {\\n      onDone?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Text mode = silent\\n    if (this.state.mode === 'text') {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Text mode, skipping TTS:', text);\\n      onDone?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (!this.init() || !this.synth) {\\n      onDone?.();\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speaking:', text);\\n    \\n    // AUDIO MUTEX: Stop listening while speaking\\n    const wasListening = this.shouldRestart;\\n    this.shouldRestart = false;\\n    if (this.recognition) {\\n      try { this.recognition.stop(); } catch (e) {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Cancel any ongoing speech\\n    this.synth.cancel();\\n    this.updateState({ audioState: 'SPEAKING' });\\n    \\n    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n    utterance.rate = 1.0;\\n    utterance.pitch = 1.0;\\n    utterance.volume = 1.0;\\n    \\n    // Get best voice\\n    const voices = this.synth.getVoices();\\n    const voice = voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Samantha')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.name.includes('Google') && v.lang.startsWith('en')) ||\\n                  voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('en-US') && !v.name.includes('Compact'));\\n    if (voice) utterance.voice = voice;\\n    \\n    utterance.onend = () => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speech ended');\\n      this.updateState({ audioState: wasListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'IDLE' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      \\n      // Resume listening if was listening before\\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    utterance.onerror = (e) => {\\n      console.log('[VoiceBrain] Speech error:', e);\\n      this.updateState({ audioState: 'IDLE' });\\n      onDone?.();\\n      \\n      if (wasListening) {\\n        this.shouldRestart = true;\\n        setTimeout(() => this.start(), 200);\\n      }\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Small delay then speak\\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      if (this.synth) {\\n        this.synth.speak(utterance);\\n      }\\n    }, 50);\\n  }\\n  \\n  stopSpeaking(): void {\\n    if (this.synth) {\\n   }\\n      if (onCommandProp) {\\n        onCommandProp(textInput.toLowerCase());\\n      }\\n      setTextInput('');\\n    }\\n  }, [textInput, onDigitsProp, onCommandProp]);\\n\\n  // Colors based from '../../../agentic';\n\ninterface Props {\n  value: string;\n  onChange: (phone: string) => void;\n  onNext: () => void;\n}\n\nconst VendorPhone: React.FC<Props> = ({ value, onChange, onNext }) => {\n  const [digits, setDigits] = useState(value.replace(/\\D/g, ''));\n\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((d: string) => {\n    setDigits(prev => {\n      const next = (prev + d).slice(0, 10);\n      onChange(next);\n      if (next.length === 10) {\n        speak(`Got it! ${formatPhone(next)}. Tell me your number again.');\n    }\n    if (cmd.includes('no') || cmd.includes('wrong')) {\n      setDigits('');\n      onChange('');\n      speak('Okay, cleared. Welcome aboard, partner.', () => onVerified());\n    } else {\n      setError('Invalid code. Demo code is 123456');\n      speak('That code is invalid. For this demo, say one two three four five six.');\n    }\n  }, [onVerified]);\n\n  const handleDigits = useCallback((digits: string) => {\n    setOtp(prev => {\n      const filled = prev.filter(d => d).length;\n      const next = [...prev];\n      let idx = filled;\n\n      for (const d of digits) {\n        if (idx < 6) {\n          next[idx] = d;\n          idx++;\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (next.filter(d => d).length === 6) {\n        setTimeout(() => verifyCode(next.join('')), 300);\n      }\n\n      return next;\n    });\n  }, [verifyCode]);\n\n  const handleCommand = useCallback((cmd: string) => {\n    if (cmd.includes('clear') || cmd.includes('reset') || cmd.includes('start over')) {\n      setOtp(['', '', '', '', '', '']);\n      setError('');\n      speak('Cleared. Go ahead with the code.');\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const u1 = onDigits(handleDigits);\n    const u2 = onCommand(handleCommand);\n    return () => { u1(); u2(); };\n  }, [handleDigits, handleCommand]);\n\n  const handleInput = (index: number, value: string) => {\n    if (!/^\\d*$/.test(value)) return;\n    const next = [...otp];\n    next[index] = value.slice(-1);\n    setOtp(next);\n    if (value && index < 5) inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();\n    if (next.every(d => d)) verifyCode(next.join(''));\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: '4em' }}>\ud83d\udd10</span>\n      <h3 style={{ color: '#B8860B', margin: '16px 0 8px', fontSize: '1.4em' }}>\n        Verification Code\n      </h3>\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: '24px' }}>\n        Code sent to {phone}\n      </p>\n\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>\n        {otp.map((digit, idx) => (\n          <input\n            key={idx}\n            ref={el => inputRefs.current[idx] = el}\n            type=\"text\"\n            inputMode=\"numeric\"\n            maxLength={1}\n            value={digit}\n            onChange={e => handleInput(idx, e.target.value)}\n            style={{\n              width: '55px',\n              height: '68px',\n              fontSize: '2em',\n              textAlign: 'center',\n              borderRadius: '12px',\n              border: `3px solid ${digit ?
